<p><b>Death Seeker</b> (デスサーチャー, <i>Desu Sāchā</i>) is a <a href="/wiki/Shadow_(Persona)" title="Shadow (Persona)">Shadow</a> in the Persona series.
</p>
<nav id="toc" class="toc" data-loaded="false"><div id="toctitle"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctoggle">[<a href="#" class="internal" id="togglelink" data-show="show" data-hide="hide">show</a>]</span></div><ol></ol></nav>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearances">Appearances</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Death_Seeker?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit Appearances section"><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" class="sprite edit-pencil" />Edit</a></span></h2>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Persona_3" title="Persona 3">Persona 3</a></i> / <i><a href="/wiki/Persona_3_FES" title="Persona 3 FES">FES</a></i> / <i><a href="/wiki/Persona_3_Portable" title="Persona 3 Portable">Portable</a></i>
</li><li><i><a href="/wiki/Persona_4" title="Persona 4">Persona 4</a></i> / <i><a href="/wiki/Persona_4_Golden" title="Persona 4 Golden">Golden</a></i>
</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Profile">Profile</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Death_Seeker?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit Profile section"><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" class="sprite edit-pencil" />Edit</a></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Persona_3"><i>Persona 3</i></span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Death_Seeker?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit Persona 3 section"><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" class="sprite edit-pencil" />Edit</a></span></h3>
<p>Death Seeker appears through the second section of the <a href="/wiki/Tziah_Block" title="Tziah Block">Tziah Block</a> within <a href="/wiki/Tartarus" title="Tartarus">Tartarus</a>, in groups of 3 or alongside <a href="/wiki/Liberating_Idol" title="Liberating Idol">Liberating Idols</a>. They will typically attack physically or use Maragion, but they will also use their Darkness skills randomly.
</p><p>Death Seekers may later be found in the second and third section of <a href="/wiki/Antenora" title="Antenora">Antenora</a> within the <a href="/wiki/Abyss_of_Time" title="Abyss of Time">Abyss of Time</a>, where they now use the Evil Smile and Mudoon skills.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Persona_4"><i>Persona 4</i></span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Death_Seeker?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit Persona 4 section"><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" class="sprite edit-pencil" />Edit</a></span></h3>
<p>Death Seekers appear on floors 1 through 4 of <a href="/wiki/Marukyu_Striptease" title="Marukyu Striptease">Marukyu Striptease</a> within the <a href="/wiki/Midnight_Channel" title="Midnight Channel">Midnight Channel</a>. In battle they will simply alternate between casting Zionga or casting Mind Charge followed by Zionga. Upon being defeated, they may drop the Iron Eyeball material. Selling 6 Iron Eyeballs at Daidara will unlock the Gothic Sword weapon for the <a href="/wiki/Yu_Narukami" title="Yu Narukami">protagonist</a> in the shop.
</p><p>In the <i>Golden</i>, it may also drop Fluorite for trade at Shiroku Pub.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Stats">Stats</span><span class="editsection"><a href="/wiki/Death_Seeker?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit Stats section"><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" class="sprite edit-pencil" />Edit</a></span></h2>
